<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SIGNATURES</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the requirements
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, the registrant has duly caused this
report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="69" height="88" src="g159761mm01i001.jpg"></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 4.0in;text-indent:-4.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 4.0in;text-indent:-4.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET CORPORATION ANNOUNCES
SECOND QUARTER EARNINGS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">MINNEAPOLIS, August&nbsp;18, 2010</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &#151; Target Corporation
(NYSE:TGT) today reported net earnings of $679 million for the quarter ended July&nbsp;31,
2010, compared with $594 million in the quarter ended August&nbsp;1, 2009.
Earnings per share in the second quarter increased 17.0 percent to 92 cents
from 79 cents in the same period a year ago. All earnings per share figures
refer to diluted earnings per share.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Our
retail segment generated strong profitability, overcoming softer-than-expected
sales,&#148; said Gregg Steinhafel, chairman, president and chief executive officer
of Target Corporation. &#147;Growth in guest traffic and apparel sales remained
robust, and teams across the company continued to exercise thoughtful control
of expenses. Our credit card segment also enjoyed very strong results, as
disciplined underwriting, superb execution and improving risk trends caused a
sharp reduction in bad debt expense compared with last year. Regardless of the
pace of recovery, we are well-positioned to continue to gain profitable market
share.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Retail Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales
increased 3.8 percent in the second quarter to $15.1 billion in 2010 from $14.6
billion in 2009, due to the contribution from new stores combined with a 1.7
percent increase in comparable-store sales. Retail segment earnings before
interest expense and income taxes (EBIT) were $1,096 million in the second
quarter of 2010, an increase of 3.1 percent from $1,064 million in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second
quarter EBITDA and EBIT margin rates were 10.5 percent and 7.2 percent,
respectively, compared with 10.6 percent and 7.3 percent in 2009. These changes
were the result of slight changes in the gross margin rate, selling, general
and administrative (SG&amp;A) expense rate, and the depreciation and
amortization (D&amp;A) expense rate.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second
quarter gross margin rate was 32.0 percent, up from 31.9 percent in 2009. The
impact of sales mix on gross margin rate was essentially neutral, as sales
increased at a similar pace in both higher-margin and lower-margin categories.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second
quarter SG&amp;A expense rate was 21.5 percent, up from 21.4 percent in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Credit Card Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second
quarter segment profit increased to $149 million from $63 million a year ago,
as bad debt expense declined 54.5 percent from $303 million in second quarter
2009 to $138 million this year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second
quarter average receivables decreased 15.1 percent to $7.1 billion in 2010 from
$8.4 billion in 2009. Average receivables directly funded by Target increased
in the second quarter to $3.0 billion from $2.9 billion in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Annualized
segment pre-tax return on invested capital was 20.2 percent in the second
quarter 2010, compared with 8.8 percent a year ago.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;more &#151;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105735\10-15976-1\task4240846\15976-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105735',CD='Aug 17 06:01 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Interest Expense and Taxes</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
interest expense for the quarter decreased $9 million from second quarter 2009,
driven by lower average debt balances partially offset by a higher average
portfolio interest rate.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
company&#146;s effective income tax rate for the second quarter was 37.2 percent in
2010, down from 37.9 percent in 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the second quarter, under the share repurchase program originally
announced in November&nbsp;2007 and resumed in January&nbsp;2010, the company
repurchased 17.5 million shares of its common stock at an average price of
$51.72, for a total investment of $907 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Program-to-date through the end of the second quarter, the company has
acquired 128.6 million shares of its common stock at an average price per share
of $51.46, reflecting a total investment of $6.6 billion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Miscellaneous</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Target Corporation will webcast its second quarter earnings conference
call at 9:30am CDT today.&#160; Investors and
the media are invited to listen to the call through the company&#146;s website at
www.target.com/investors (click on &#147;events + presentations&#148; and then &#147;archives
+ webcasts&#148;). A telephone replay of the call will be available beginning at
approximately 11:30am CDT today through the end of business on August&nbsp;20,
2010. The replay number is (800) 642-1687 (passcode: 49644107).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Target Corporation&#146;s retail segment includes large general merchandise
and food discount stores and Target.com, a fully integrated on-line business.
In addition, the company operates a credit card segment that offers branded
proprietary credit card products. The company currently operates 1,743 Target
stores in 49 states.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Target Corporation news releases are available at www.target.com.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TARGET CORPORATION</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated Statements of Financial Position</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="55%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:55.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">EBITDA is earnings before interest expense, income
taxes, depreciation and amortization.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">EBIT is earnings before interest expense and income
taxes.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(a)&nbsp;New account and loyalty rewards redeemed by
our guests reduce reported sales. Our Retail Segment charges the cost of these
discounts to our Credit Card Segment, and the reimbursements of $17 million and
$34 million for the three and six months ended July&nbsp;31, 2010,
respectively, and $21 million and $41 million for the three and six months
ended August&nbsp;1, 2009, respectively, are recorded as a reduction to
SG&amp;A expenses within the Retail Segment.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(a)&nbsp;New account and loyalty rewards redeemed by our
guests reduce reported sales. Our Retail Segment charges the cost of these
discounts to our Credit Card Segment, and the reimbursements of $17 million and
$34 million for the three and six months ended July&nbsp;31, 2010,
respectively, and $21 million and $41 million for the three and six months
ended August&nbsp;1, 2009, respectively, are recorded as an increase to
Operations and Marketing expenses within the Credit Card Segment.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(b)&nbsp;Amounts represent the portion of average credit
card receivables funded by Target. These amounts exclude $4,148 million and
$4,667 million for the three and six months ended July&nbsp;31, 2010,
respectively, and $5,508 million and $5,502 million for the three and six
months ended August&nbsp;1, 2009, respectively, of receivables funded by
nonrecourse debt collateralized by credit card receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(c)&nbsp;ROIC is return on invested capital, and this rate
represents segment profit divided by average receivables funded by Target,
expressed as an annualized rate.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(d)&nbsp;As an annualized percentage of average gross credit
card receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(a)&nbsp;Balance-weighted average one-month LIBOR</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(b)&nbsp;As a percentage of average gross credit card
receivables.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(c)&nbsp;Spread to LIBOR is a metric used to analyze the
performance of our total credit card portfolio because the vast majority of our
portfolio earns finance charge revenue at rates tied to the Prime Rate, and the
interest rate on all nonrecourse debt securitized by credit card receivables is
tied to LIBOR.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Rollforward Analysis</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(a)&nbsp;Net write-offs include the principal amount
of losses (excluding accrued and unpaid finance charges) less current period
principal recoveries.</font></i></p>
